            (1): Dropout(p=0.0, inplace=False)
            (2): Sequential(
              (0): TransposeLast()
              (1): Fp32LayerNorm((512,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
              (2): TransposeLast()
            )
            (3): GELU(approximate='none')
          )
          (5-6): 2 x Sequential(

        (0): TransposeLast()
        (1): Sequential(
